### 2.2 S√©paration des responsabilit√©s

| Module  | Responsabilit√©                                           | Tables principales                                           |
| ------- | -------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------ |
| **CRM** | Acquisition prospects ‚Üí clients                          | crm_leads, crm_quotes, crm_orders, crm_activities            |
| **CLT** | Gestion compte client (masterdata, facturation, membres) | clt_masterdata, clt_members, clt_invoices, clt_subscriptions |
| **ADM** | Infrastructure technique tenant + config syst√®me         | adm_tenants, adm_providers, adm_roles                        |

### 2.3 Principe de s√©paration CLT vs ADM

**CLT = Donn√©es m√©tier du client**

- Qui est le client (identit√©, contacts, historique)
- Sa facturation (invoices, subscriptions)
- Ses utilisateurs (members)

**ADM = Configuration technique du tenant**

- Liaison Clerk Organization
- Timezone, currency, country
- Subdomain, status technique

### 3.2 D√©tail des statuts

| Statut            | Phase         | Description                         | D√©clencheur     | Probabilit√© |
| ----------------- | ------------- | ----------------------------------- | --------------- | ----------- |
| `new`             | Acquisition   | Email entr√©, pas de booking Cal.com | Wizard √©tape 1  | 5%          |
| `demo_scheduled`  | Acquisition   | Cr√©neau Cal.com confirm√©            | Webhook Cal.com | 50%         |
| `qualified`       | Qualification | Qualifi√© CPT pendant l'appel        | Commercial      | 70%         |
| `demo_completed`  | Demo          | Demo r√©alis√©e, en attente d√©cision  | Commercial      | 75%         |
| `proposal_sent`   | Closing       | Lien paiement Stripe g√©n√©r√©         | Commercial      | 85%         |
| `payment_pending` | Closing       | Lien envoy√©, attente paiement       | Commercial      | 90%         |
| `converted`       | R√©sultat      | Paiement re√ßu, tenant cr√©√©          | Stripe webhook  | 100%        |
| `lost`            | R√©sultat      | Perdu d√©finitivement                | Commercial      | 0%          |
| `nurturing`       | R√©sultat      | Timing pas bon, relance programm√©e  | Commercial      | 15%         |
| `disqualified`    | R√©sultat      | Hors cible / Red flag               | Commercial      | 0%          |

### 3.3 Transitions autoris√©es

```
new ‚Üí demo_scheduled | disqualified

demo_scheduled ‚Üí qualified | nurturing | lost | disqualified

qualified ‚Üí demo_completed | lost

demo_completed ‚Üí proposal_sent | nurturing | lost

proposal_sent ‚Üí payment_pending | lost | nurturing

payment_pending ‚Üí converted | lost

converted ‚Üí (terminal)

lost ‚Üí nurturing (si recovery possible)

nurturing ‚Üí demo_scheduled (si recontact)

disqualified ‚Üí (terminal)
```

### 3.4 Raisons de cl√¥ture (obligatoires)

**Pour `lost`** :

- `not_interested` - Pas int√©ress√©
- `chose_competitor` - A choisi un concurrent (competitor_name requis)
- `price_perception` - Prix per√ßu comme trop √©lev√©
- `bad_timing` - Mauvais timing
- `no_response` - Ne r√©pond plus
- `no_show` - Ne s'est pas pr√©sent√© au RDV

**Pour `disqualified`** :

- `wrong_segment` - Mauvais segment
- `wrong_country` - Pays non couvert
- `spam_fake` - Spam ou faux lead
- `duplicate` - Doublon
- `test_lead` - Lead de test

| Aspect            | Valeur                                                                                         |
| ----------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Produit**       | App mobile (iOS + Android)                                                                     |
| **Mod√®le**        | Freemium ‚Üí 1 MOIS SATISFAIT/REMBOURS√â                                                          |
| **Page d'entr√©e** | /solopreneur (vid√©o d√©mo + liens stores)                                                       |
| **CRM**           | ‚ùå Non applicable - Product Analytics (Mixpanel)                                               |
| **Raison**        | Les modules SaaS (recrutement drivers, gestion flottes) ne sont pas pertinents pour 1 v√©hicule |

### 4.3 Segments 2-4 : Flottes (2+ v√©hicules)

| Segment                 | Taille          | Processus                      | Escalade DG                     |
| ----------------------- | --------------- | ------------------------------ | ------------------------------- |
| **Segment 2 - Starter** | 2-9 v√©hicules   | Wizard ‚Üí 1 appel ‚Üí Conversion  | Non                             |
| **Segment 3 - Pro**     | 10-49 v√©hicules | Wizard ‚Üí 1 appel ‚Üí Conversion  | Non                             |
| **Segment 4 - Premium** | 50+ v√©hicules   | Wizard ‚Üí Appel ‚Üí Quote si n√©go | Oui (param√©trable, d√©faut: 20+) |

**Note importante :** Le seuil d'escalade DG est param√©trable dans `crm_settings` (cl√©: `escalation_fleet_threshold`, d√©faut: 20).

**Sp√©cifications techniques :**

| Champ            | Type     | Obligatoire  | Validation                         |
| ---------------- | -------- | ------------ | ---------------------------------- |
| `first_name`     | String   | ‚úÖ Oui       | Min 2 caract√®res                   |
| `last_name`      | String   | ‚úÖ Oui       | Min 2 caract√®res                   |
| `company_name`   | String   | ‚úÖ Oui       | Min 2 caract√®res                   |
| `fleet_size`     | Enum     | ‚úÖ Oui       | `2-9` / `10-49` / `50-99` / `100+` |
| `country_code`   | String   | ‚úÖ Oui       | ISO 3166-1 alpha-2                 |
| `phone`          | String   | ‚úÖ Oui       | libphonenumber-js validation       |
| `platforms_used` | String[] | ‚ùå Non       | Multi-select checkbox              |
| `terms_accepted` | Boolean  | ‚úÖ Oui       | Must be true                       |
| `gdpr_consent`   | Boolean  | Conditionnel | Si country_code in EU/EEA          |

**Validation t√©l√©phone :**

```typescript
import { isValidPhoneNumber, parsePhoneNumber } from "libphonenumber-js";

const isValid = isValidPhoneNumber(phone, countryCode);
const parsed = parsePhoneNumber(phone, countryCode);
const formatted = parsed.formatInternational(); // +971 50 123 4567
```

**Comportement :**

- Submit ‚Üí Update lead avec toutes les infos, `wizard_completed = TRUE`
- **SANS t√©l√©phone = PAS DE CONFIRMATION** (bouton d√©sactiv√©)

### 5.6 Responsive Design

| Breakpoint          | Layout                                       |
| ------------------- | -------------------------------------------- |
| Desktop (>1024px)   | Wizard centr√©, calendrier large              |
| Tablet (768-1024px) | Wizard full-width, calendrier adapt√©         |
| Mobile (<768px)     | Wizard stack vertical, calendrier scrollable |

**Mobile sp√©cifique :**

- Progress bar fixe en haut
- Boutons Continue/Back sticky en bas
- Calendrier avec scroll horizontal si n√©cessaire

## 6. INT√âGRATION CAL.COM

### 6.1 Pourquoi Cal.com ?

| Crit√®re           | Cal.com             | Calendly       |
| ----------------- | ------------------- | -------------- |
| **Prix**          | Free plan suffisant | $10+/user/mois |
| **Embed**         | ‚úÖ React SDK natif  | ‚úÖ Embed JS    |
| **Webhooks**      | ‚úÖ Inclus           | ‚úÖ Payant      |
| **Customisation** | ‚úÖ Open source      | ‚ö†Ô∏è Limit√©e     |

**D√©cision : Cal.com Free est suffisant pour notre usage**

### 6.2 Configuration Cal.com

| Param√®tre       | Valeur                              |
| --------------- | ----------------------------------- |
| **Plan**        | Free ($0/mois)                      |
| **Commerciaux** | 1 au d√©marrage                      |
| **Routing**     | Non (distribution interne manuelle) |
| **Event Type**  | "FleetCore Demo Call"               |

### 6.3 Event Type : "FleetCore Demo Call"

| Param√®tre       | Valeur                   | Justification                               |
| --------------- | ------------------------ | ------------------------------------------- |
| Duration        | 30 minutes               | Qual (5) + Demo (15) + Closing (5) + buffer |
| Buffer before   | 5 minutes                | Pr√©paration commercial                      |
| Buffer after    | 10 minutes               | Notes + CRM update                          |
| Minimum notice  | 4 hours                  | √âviter bookings trop proches                |
| Slots increment | 30 minutes               | Cr√©neaux propres                            |
| Availability    | Lun-Ven 9h-18h           | Heures business                             |
| Timezone        | UAE (GST) / France (CET) | Selon commercial                            |

### 6.4 Embed React

```tsx
// components/booking/CalEmbed.tsx
import Cal, { getCalApi } from "@calcom/embed-react";
import { useEffect } from "react";

interface CalEmbedProps {
  email: string;
  onBookingComplete: (booking: CalBookingData) => void;
  onError: (error: Error) => void;
}

interface CalBookingData {
  uid: string;
  startTime: string;
  endTime: string;
  attendees: Array<{ email: string; name: string }>;
}

export function CalEmbed({ email, onBookingComplete, onError }: CalEmbedProps) {
  useEffect(() => {
    (async function () {
      const cal = await getCalApi();

      // Styling
      cal("ui", {
        styles: {
          branding: { brandColor: "#0066FF" },
        },
        hideEventTypeDetails: false,
      });

      // Event handlers
      cal("on", {
        action: "bookingSuccessful",
        callback: (e: { detail: { data: CalBookingData } }) => {
          onBookingComplete(e.detail.data);
        },
      });

      cal("on", {
        action: "bookingFailed",
        callback: (e: { detail: { error: Error } }) => {
          onError(e.detail.error);
        },
      });
    })();
  }, [onBookingComplete, onError]);

  return (
    <Cal
      calLink="fleetcore/demo"
      style={{ width: "100%", height: "500px", overflow: "scroll" }}
      config={{
        email: email,
        name: "",
        layout: "month_view",
      }}
    />
  );
}
```

### 6.5 Webhooks Cal.com ‚Üí FleetCore

| Event Cal.com         | Endpoint FleetCore              | Action                                                            |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `booking.created`     | `POST /api/crm/webhooks/calcom` | Update lead status ‚Üí `demo_scheduled`, store `booking_calcom_uid` |
| `booking.rescheduled` | `POST /api/crm/webhooks/calcom` | Update `booking_slot_at`, log activity                            |
| `booking.cancelled`   | `POST /api/crm/webhooks/calcom` | Update lead status ‚Üí `lost` (reason: cancelled_by_prospect)       |

**Webhook handler :**

```typescript
// app/api/crm/webhooks/calcom/route.ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { verifyCalcomWebhook } from "@/lib/calcom";
import { leadService } from "@/services/crm/lead.service";

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const body = await req.json();
  const signature = req.headers.get("x-cal-signature");

  // Verify webhook signature
  if (!verifyCalcomWebhook(body, signature)) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "Invalid signature" }, { status: 401 });
  }

  const { triggerEvent, payload } = body;

  switch (triggerEvent) {
    case "BOOKING_CREATED":
      await handleBookingCreated(payload);
      break;
    case "BOOKING_RESCHEDULED":
      await handleBookingRescheduled(payload);
      break;
    case "BOOKING_CANCELLED":
      await handleBookingCancelled(payload);
      break;
  }

  return NextResponse.json({ received: true });
}

async function handleBookingCreated(payload: CalBookingPayload) {
  const { uid, startTime, attendees } = payload;
  const email = attendees[0]?.email;

  if (!email) return;

  // Find lead by email and update
  await leadService.updateByEmail(email, {
    status: "demo_scheduled",
    booking_slot_at: new Date(startTime),
    booking_calcom_uid: uid,
  });

  // Log activity
  await leadService.logActivity(email, {
    activity_type: "booking_created",
    title: "Demo scheduled via Cal.com",
    metadata: { calcom_uid: uid, start_time: startTime },
  });
}
```

### 6.6 Cal.com Workflows (automatiques)

| Workflow     | Trigger           | Action                                            |
| ------------ | ----------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| Confirmation | `booking.created` | Email confirmation au prospect (Cal.com template) |
| Reminder 1h  | 1h before booking | Email reminder au prospect (Cal.com template)     |

**Note :** L'email J-1 avec boutons Confirm/Reschedule est g√©r√© par FleetCore (voir section 10).

## 7. PROCESSUS APPEL COMMERCIAL

### 7.1 Philosophie : One-Call Close

> "L'appel n'est PAS un appel de qualification suivi d'une demo s√©par√©e. C'est UN SEUL appel o√π on qualifie, on d√©montre, et on close."

**Pourquoi one-call close :**

| Argument              | Explication                                      |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------------------------ |
| **Cycle court**       | Flottes VTC = d√©cideur unique, pas de comit√©     |
| **Produit vertical**  | FleetCore r√©sout un probl√®me sp√©cifique et clair |
| **Moins de friction** | 2 appels = 50% de perte entre chaque             |
| **Momentum**          | Prospect chaud = closing imm√©diat                |

### 7.2 R√®gles strictes

| R√®gle                       | Description                                                        | Cons√©quence si non respect√©e |
| --------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------ | ---------------------------- |
| **Appel √† l'heure exacte**  | Le commercial appelle √† l'heure book√©e, pas avant, pas apr√®s       | Perte de cr√©dibilit√©         |
| **Pas de "je rappelle"**    | Si pas de r√©ponse ‚Üí 2 tentatives espac√©es de 5 min, puis SMS/email | Lead ‚Üí lost                  |
| **Pas de n√©gociation prix** | Prix fixe. Satisfait/rembours√© 30 jours = la seule concession      | D√©valuation du produit       |
| **Closing dans l'appel**    | Si qualifi√©, le deal se ferme PENDANT l'appel                      | Lead ‚Üí nurturing             |

## 8. FRAMEWORK QUALIFICATION CPT

### 8.1 Pourquoi CPT ? (pas CHAMP/BANT)

**Contexte FleetCore :**

| Contexte                    | Implication                                          |
| --------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------- |
| Appel **INBOUND**           | Le prospect a demand√© la demo ‚Üí d√©j√† int√©ress√©       |
| **D√©cideur** au t√©l√©phone   | Celui qui booke = celui qui d√©cide (petites flottes) |
| **Pas de n√©gociation** prix | On affirme le ROI, on ne demande pas le budget       |
| **Cycle court**             | Pas besoin de qualifier 50 personnes                 |

**Questions BANT/CHAMP SUPPRIM√âES :**

| Question                                            | Pourquoi supprim√©e                          |
| --------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------- |
| **Authority** : "C'est vous qui d√©cidez ?"          | Ridicule en inbound - c'est lui qui a book√© |
| **Money/Budget** : "√áa correspond √† votre budget ?" | Position de faiblesse - on affirme le ROI   |
| **Need** (BANT)                                     | Trop vague - CPT est plus pr√©cis            |

### 8.2 Les 3 Questions CPT

```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ                       FRAMEWORK CPT                                         ‚îÇ
```

### 8.3 Matrice de d√©cision GO/NO-GO

```

‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§

‚îÇ  HIGH       ‚îÇ HIGH     ‚îÇ HOT    ‚îÇ ‚úÖ PERFECT FIT    ‚îÇ Close imm√©diat       ‚îÇ
```

| --------------------------------- | -------------------- | ----------------------- |
| "Je cherche du gratuit"           | STOP - Disqualifi√©   | Pas le bon segment      |
| "Je dois en parler √† mon associ√©" | Nurturing            | Pas le d√©cideur         |
| "Combien √ßa co√ªte ?" (en premier) | R√©pondre + qualifier | Prix-focused = red flag |
| "Je veux juste voir"              | Qualifier davantage  | Tire-kicker potentiel   |
| Pas de douleur identifiable       | Nurturing            | Pas de besoin r√©el      |

### 8.5 Stockage des r√©ponses CPT

**Utiliser les colonnes EXISTANTES de `crm_leads` :**

| Donn√©e              | Colonne existante     | Type            |
| ------------------- | --------------------- | --------------- |
| Score global        | `qualification_score` | integer (0-100) |
| Notes de l'appel    | `qualification_notes` | text            |
| Date qualification  | `qualified_date`      | timestamptz     |
| D√©tail r√©ponses CPT | `scoring`             | jsonb           |

**Format du jsonb `scoring` :**


## 9. DISCOURS COMMERCIAL (STYLE GRIDWISE)

### 9.1 Philosophie

**Ce que fait Gridwise (et qu'on copie) :**

| √âl√©ment  | Gridwise          | FleetCore                          |
| -------- | ----------------- | ---------------------------------- |
| Focus    | GAIN, pas co√ªt    | GAIN, pas co√ªt                     |
| Promesse | "Earn 30% more"   | "Earn more within first month"     |
| Preuve   | "500K drivers"    | "Flottes comme la v√¥tre"           |
| Prix     | Jamais en premier | Affirm√© en closing, pas questionn√© |

**Ce que Gridwise ne fait JAMAIS (et nous non plus) :**

- "√áa correspond √† votre budget ?"
- "Est-ce que le prix vous convient ?"
- "Vous avez des questions sur le tarif ?"
- Position d√©fensive sur le prix

| "Need to reschedule" | Redirect vers `https://cal.com/fleetcore/demo/reschedule/{uid}`               |

### 10.5 Template email (React Email)

## 11. MODULE CLT - CLIENT

### 11.1 P√©rim√®tre

Le module CLT g√®re **le compte client** apr√®s conversion. C'est le "Customer Account" avec toutes les donn√©es m√©tier du client.

### 11.2 Tables CLT (renommage + cr√©ation)

| Table V6.2          | Ex-table                 | Action   | Description                               |
| ------------------- | ------------------------ | -------- | ----------------------------------------- |
| `clt_masterdata`    | NOUVELLE                 | CR√âER    | Donn√©es identit√© client + historique lead |
| `clt_members`       | adm_members              | RENOMMER | Utilisateurs du client                    |
| `clt_invoices`      | bil_tenant_invoices      | RENOMMER | Factures √©mises au client                 |
| `clt_invoice_lines` | bil_tenant_invoice_lines | RENOMMER | Lignes de factures                        |
| `clt_subscriptions` | bil_tenant_subscriptions | RENOMMER | Abonnements actifs                        |

### 11.3 Table clt_masterdata (NOUVELLE)

```sql
CREATE TABLE clt_masterdata (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),

  -- Lien technique
  tenant_id UUID NOT NULL UNIQUE REFERENCES adm_tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  provider_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES adm_providers(id),

  -- Code client unique (g√©n√©r√© automatiquement)
  customer_code VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE, -- Format: CLT-XXXXXX

  -- Audit trail CRM (IMPORTANT: lien historique)
  origin_lead_id UUID REFERENCES crm_leads(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  origin_lead_code VARCHAR(50), -- Copie du lead_code pour r√©f√©rence m√™me si lead supprim√©

  -- Identit√© entreprise (transf√©r√© depuis crm_leads)
  company_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  legal_name TEXT, -- Raison sociale officielle
  registration_number VARCHAR(50), -- SIRET, CR, etc.
  vat_number VARCHAR(50),

  -- Coordonn√©es (transf√©r√© depuis crm_leads)
  email TEXT NOT NULL,
  phone VARCHAR(50),
  website_url TEXT,
  linkedin_url TEXT,

  -- Adresse principale
  address_line1 TEXT,
  address_line2 TEXT,
  city TEXT,
  postal_code VARCHAR(20),
  country_code CHAR(2) NOT NULL,

  -- Contact principal
  primary_contact_first_name TEXT,
  primary_contact_last_name TEXT,
  primary_contact_email TEXT,
  primary_contact_phone VARCHAR(50),
  primary_contact_role VARCHAR(100), -- CEO, Fleet Manager, etc.

  -- Caract√©ristiques business
  fleet_size INTEGER,
  industry TEXT,
  segment VARCHAR(20), -- starter, pro, premium

  -- Dates cl√©s
  customer_since DATE NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_DATE,

  -- M√©tadonn√©es
  metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,

  -- Audit standard
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  created_by UUID,
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_by UUID,
  deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  deleted_by UUID,
  deletion_reason TEXT
);

-- Indexes
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX idx_clt_masterdata_customer_code ON clt_masterdata(customer_code);
CREATE INDEX idx_clt_masterdata_tenant ON clt_masterdata(tenant_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_clt_masterdata_origin_lead ON clt_masterdata(origin_lead_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_clt_masterdata_country ON clt_masterdata(country_code);
CREATE INDEX idx_clt_masterdata_segment ON clt_masterdata(segment);

-- Trigger updated_at
CREATE TRIGGER set_updated_at_clt_masterdata
  BEFORE UPDATE ON clt_masterdata
  FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION trigger_set_updated_at();

-- Trigger g√©n√©ration customer_code
CREATE TRIGGER trg_set_customer_code
  BEFORE INSERT ON clt_masterdata
  FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION set_customer_code();
```

### 11.4 Fonction g√©n√©ration customer_code

```sql
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION set_customer_code()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
DECLARE
  next_val INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF NEW.customer_code IS NULL THEN
    -- R√©cup√©rer et incr√©menter la s√©quence
    UPDATE crm_sequences
    SET current_value = current_value + 1
    WHERE entity_type = 'customer'
    RETURNING current_value INTO next_val;

    -- Si pas de s√©quence, la cr√©er
    IF next_val IS NULL THEN
      INSERT INTO crm_sequences (entity_type, prefix, current_value, padding)
      VALUES ('customer', 'CLT', 1, 6)
      RETURNING current_value INTO next_val;
    END IF;

    NEW.customer_code := 'CLT-' || LPAD(next_val::TEXT, 6, '0');
  END IF;
  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;
```

### 11.5 Renommage tables existantes

```sql
-- clt_members (ex adm_members)
ALTER TABLE adm_members RENAME TO clt_members;

-- clt_invoices (ex bil_tenant_invoices)
ALTER TABLE bil_tenant_invoices RENAME TO clt_invoices;

-- clt_invoice_lines (ex bil_tenant_invoice_lines)
ALTER TABLE bil_tenant_invoice_lines RENAME TO clt_invoice_lines;

-- clt_subscriptions (ex bil_tenant_subscriptions)
ALTER TABLE bil_tenant_subscriptions RENAME TO clt_subscriptions;

-- Mettre √† jour les FK dans clt_invoice_lines
ALTER TABLE clt_invoice_lines
  DROP CONSTRAINT bil_tenant_invoice_lines_invoice_id_fkey,
  ADD CONSTRAINT clt_invoice_lines_invoice_id_fkey
    FOREIGN KEY (invoice_id) REFERENCES clt_invoices(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;
```

## 12. MODULE ADM - TENANT

### 12.1 P√©rim√®tre r√©vis√©

Apr√®s refactoring, `adm_tenants` se concentre sur :

- Liaison technique avec Clerk Organization
- Configuration technique (timezone, currency, subdomain)
- Statut technique du tenant

### 12.2 Table adm_tenants simplifi√©e

Les colonnes m√©tier client sont d√©plac√©es vers `clt_masterdata` :

| Colonne                 | Destination                          | Raison        |
| ----------------------- | ------------------------------------ | ------------- |
| `name`                  | clt_masterdata.company_name          | Donn√©e client |
| `country_code`          | clt_masterdata.country_code          | Donn√©e client |
| `vat_rate`              | clt_masterdata (√† calculer)          | Donn√©e client |
| `primary_contact_email` | clt_masterdata.primary_contact_email | Donn√©e client |
| `primary_contact_phone` | clt_masterdata.primary_contact_phone | Donn√©e client |
| `billing_email`         | clt_masterdata.email                 | Donn√©e client |

**Colonnes CONSERV√âES dans adm_tenants** :

- `id`, `clerk_organization_id`, `subdomain`
- `default_currency`, `timezone`
- `status`, `onboarding_completed_at`, `trial_ends_at`, `next_invoice_date`
- `tenant_code`, `created_at`, `updated_at`, `deleted_at`

```
     ‚îÇ                                    ‚îÇ
     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

### 13.2 √âtape 1 - G√©n√©ration lien paiement

**Acteur:** Commercial FleetCore

**Pr√©requis:** Lead avec status IN (qualified, demo_completed, proposal_sent)

**Flow:**

```
Lead (status=proposal_sent)
       ‚îÇ
       ‚îÇ Commercial clique "G√©n√©rer lien paiement"
       ‚ñº
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ POST /api/v1/bil/payment-links                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îú‚îÄ‚ñ∫ V√©rifier status autoris√© (depuis bil_settings)                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îú‚îÄ‚ñ∫ D√©terminer segment via crm_settings.segment_thresholds                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îú‚îÄ‚ñ∫ Stripe: createCheckoutSession()                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ     - mode: subscription                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ     - discounts: [{ coupon: FIRST_MONTH_FREE }]                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ     - metadata: { lead_id, lead_code, performed_by }                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ     - expires_at: NOW() + expiry_hours (depuis bil_settings)               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îú‚îÄ‚ñ∫ Update lead:                                                             ‚îÇ

‚îÇ ‚îî‚îÄ‚ñ∫ Return: { payment_url, session_id, expires_at }                          ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

### 13.3 √âtape 2 - Paiement + Conversion automatique

**Acteur:** Client + Webhook Stripe

**Flow:**

```

       ‚îÇ
       ‚ñº
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ WEBHOOK: checkout.session.completed                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ TRANSACTION ATOMIQUE:                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îú‚îÄ‚ñ∫ 1. Cr√©er adm_tenants                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ       - status = "pending_verification"                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ       - stripe_customer_id, stripe_subscription_id                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ       - verification_token (expire 24h)                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ       - clerk_organization_id = NULL (pas encore)                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ                                                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îú‚îÄ‚ñ∫ 2. Cr√©er organisation Clerk                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ‚îÇ       - Clerk API: createOrganization()                                    ‚îÇ
```

### 13.4 √âtape 3 - Formulaire v√©rification client

**Acteur:** Client (page publique)

**Route:** `/[locale]/verify?token=xxx`

**Conditions d'acc√®s:**

- Token valide (existe en DB)
- Token non expir√© (< 24h)
- Token non utilis√© (verification_completed_at IS NULL)

**Formulaire:**


**Actions POST /api/public/verify:**

- Valider token
- Update adm_tenants (donn√©es soci√©t√© + admin_name + admin_email)

- Update clt_masterdata (donn√©es soci√©t√©)
- Trigger invitation admin (√©tape 4)

### 13.6 1er mois gratuit (pas trial)

**Justification business:**

| Aspect            | Trial 14-30j         | 1er mois gratuit ‚úÖ    |
| ----------------- | -------------------- | ---------------------- |
| **CB requise**    | Non                  | **Oui**                |
| **Statut client** | "En test"            | **Client d√®s jour 1**  |
| **√Ä la fin**      | Doit AGIR pour payer | Doit AGIR pour annuler |
| **Conversion**    | 15-25%               | **60-80%**             |

**Impl√©mentation Stripe:**

```javascript

// duration: 'once' dans config Stripe Dashboard
```

### 14.3 Modification crm_quotes

```sql
-- Ajout lead_id (en plus de opportunity_id existant)
ALTER TABLE crm_quotes ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS lead_id UUID REFERENCES crm_leads(id) ON DELETE SET NULL;

-- Contrainte XOR lead/opportunity
ALTER TABLE crm_quotes
  ADD CONSTRAINT crm_quotes_lead_or_opportunity_xor
  CHECK (
    (lead_id IS NOT NULL AND opportunity_id IS NULL) OR
    (lead_id IS NULL AND opportunity_id IS NOT NULL)
  );

-- Index
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crm_quotes_lead ON crm_quotes(lead_id) WHERE lead_id IS NOT NULL;
```

### 14.4 Escalade DG

| √âl√©ment         | Valeur                                                                       |
| --------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Seuil**       | Param√©trable dans `crm_settings.escalation_fleet_threshold` (d√©faut: 20)     |
| **D√©clencheur** | Prospect Segment 4 veut n√©gocier le tarif                                    |
| **Canal**       | Email (pas dans l'application)                                               |
| **Responsable** | DG directement                                                               |
| **Signalement** | Si non mis √† jour apr√®s `escalation_alert_hours` (param√©trable, d√©faut: 48h) |

## 15. OPPORTUNITY PIPELINE (FREEZE)

### 15.1 Statut actuel

**FREEZE** - Le module Opportunity n'est pas utilis√© pour l'acquisition initiale.

### 15.2 Utilisation future

Le module Opportunity sera utilis√© pour :

- Upsell de modules additionnels aux clients existants
- Vente d'addons (carte zones rentables, analytics avanc√©s, etc.)

### 15.3 Point de d√©part futur

L'Opportunity d√©marrera depuis le **compte client** (clt_masterdata), pas depuis un Lead.

```
[Client existant (clt_masterdata)]
         ‚îÇ
         ‚ñº
crm_opportunities (pour addon/module)
         ‚îÇ
         ‚ñº
crm_quotes (opportunity_id = ...)
         ‚îÇ
         ‚ñº
crm_orders (additionnel)
```

### 15.4 Tables concern√©es

- `crm_opportunities` - Pas de modification, pas d'utilisation pour le moment
- `crm_pipelines` - Idem
- `crm_opportunity_stages` - Idem

### 16.2 Leviers commerciaux autoris√©s

| -------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------- |
| **+1 mois gratuit (n√©go)**       | Commercial (Segments 2-3 si insistant) | Via discount visible dans fiche Lead                       |
| **+1 mois gratuit (parrainage)** | Automatique si parrain valide          | `crm_referrals.referrer_reward_applied_at`                 |
| **Quote avec avantages**         | Commercial (Segment 4)                 | `crm_quotes.free_months`, `crm_quotes.free_vehicles_count` |

**Note :** Les colonnes de tracking suppl√©mentaires ne sont pas n√©cessaires car le discount attribu√© et le nom du commercial sont d√©j√† visibles dans la fiche Lead pour r√©conciliation.

## 17. MODIFICATIONS SCHEMA V6.2.1

### 17.1 Migration crm_leads

```sql
-- =============================================================================
-- FLEETCORE CRM V6.2.1 - MIGRATION LEADS
-- Date: 2026-01-06
-- Description: 10 statuts (+payment_pending), colonnes booking Cal.com, Stripe
-- =============================================================================

BEGIN;

-- 1. Nouvelles colonnes booking Cal.com
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS booking_slot_at TIMESTAMPTZ;
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS booking_confirmed_at TIMESTAMPTZ;
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS booking_calcom_uid VARCHAR(100);
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS platforms_used TEXT[];

COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.booking_slot_at IS 'V6.2: Date/heure du cr√©neau Cal.com';
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.booking_confirmed_at IS 'V6.2: Date confirmation email J-1';
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.booking_calcom_uid IS 'V6.2: UID booking Cal.com';
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.platforms_used IS 'V6.2: Plateformes VTC (Uber, Bolt, etc.)';

-- 2. Colonne wizard_completed
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS wizard_completed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE;

COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.wizard_completed IS 'V6.2: TRUE si √©tape 3 wizard compl√©t√©e (t√©l√©phone fourni)';

-- 3. Colonne lien tenant
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS tenant_id UUID REFERENCES adm_tenants(id);
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS converted_at TIMESTAMPTZ;

COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.tenant_id IS 'V6.2: R√©f√©rence vers tenant cr√©√© apr√®s conversion';
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.converted_at IS 'V6.2: Date/heure de conversion';

-- 4. V6.2.1: Colonnes Stripe Payment Link
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS stripe_checkout_session_id VARCHAR(255);
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS stripe_payment_link_url TEXT;
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS payment_link_created_at TIMESTAMPTZ;
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS payment_link_expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ;

COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.stripe_checkout_session_id IS 'V6.2.1: Stripe Checkout Session ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.stripe_payment_link_url IS 'V6.2.1: URL lien paiement envoy√©';
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.payment_link_created_at IS 'V6.2.1: Date cr√©ation lien paiement';
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.payment_link_expires_at IS 'V6.2.1: Date expiration lien paiement';

-- 5. Index
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crm_leads_booking_slot
ON crm_leads(booking_slot_at)
WHERE booking_slot_at IS NOT NULL;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crm_leads_booking_calcom_uid
ON crm_leads(booking_calcom_uid)
WHERE booking_calcom_uid IS NOT NULL;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crm_leads_wizard_completed
ON crm_leads(wizard_completed);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crm_leads_tenant
ON crm_leads(tenant_id)
WHERE tenant_id IS NOT NULL;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crm_leads_stripe_checkout
ON crm_leads(stripe_checkout_session_id)
WHERE stripe_checkout_session_id IS NOT NULL;

-- 6. Mise √† jour CHECK constraint status (10 statuts V6.2.1)

-- D'abord, migrer les anciens statuts si pr√©sents
UPDATE crm_leads SET status = 'new' WHERE status = 'demo_requested';

-- Supprimer ancienne contrainte
ALTER TABLE crm_leads DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS crm_leads_status_check;

-- Nouvelle contrainte avec 10 statuts V6.2.1
ALTER TABLE crm_leads ADD CONSTRAINT crm_leads_status_check
CHECK (status IN (
  'new',
  'demo_scheduled',
  'qualified',
  'demo_completed',
  'proposal_sent',
  'payment_pending',
  'converted',
  'lost',
  'nurturing',
  'disqualified'
));

-- 7. Marquer colonnes deprecated
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.callback_requested_at IS 'DEPRECATED V6.2 - Flux callback supprim√©';
COMMENT ON COLUMN crm_leads.callback_scheduled_at IS 'DEPRECATED V6.2 - Flux callback supprim√©';

-- 8. Commentaire table
COMMENT ON TABLE crm_leads IS 'V6.2.1: Leads CRM - 10 statuts, wizard booking, Stripe payment flow';

COMMIT;
```

### 17.2 Migration adm_tenants (V6.2.1)

```sql
-- =============================================================================
-- FLEETCORE V6.2.1 - MIGRATION ADM_TENANTS
-- Date: 2026-01-06
-- Description: Colonnes Stripe, v√©rification client, admin d√©sign√©, CGI
-- =============================================================================

BEGIN;

-- 1. Colonnes Stripe
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS stripe_customer_id VARCHAR(255);
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS stripe_subscription_id VARCHAR(255);

COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.stripe_customer_id IS 'V6.2.1: Stripe Customer ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.stripe_subscription_id IS 'V6.2.1: Stripe Subscription ID';

-- 2. Colonnes v√©rification client (lien 24h)
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS verification_token VARCHAR(100);
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS verification_token_expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ;
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS verification_completed_at TIMESTAMPTZ;

COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.verification_token IS 'V6.2.1: Token v√©rification email (24h)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.verification_token_expires_at IS 'V6.2.1: Expiration token v√©rification';
COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.verification_completed_at IS 'V6.2.1: Date compl√©tion v√©rification';

-- 3. Colonnes admin d√©sign√© par le client
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS admin_name VARCHAR(255);
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS admin_email VARCHAR(255);
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS admin_invited_at TIMESTAMPTZ;

COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.admin_name IS 'V6.2.1: Nom admin d√©sign√© par client';
COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.admin_email IS 'V6.2.1: Email admin d√©sign√© par client';
COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.admin_invited_at IS 'V6.2.1: Date envoi invitation Clerk';

-- 4. Colonnes CGI / CGU
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS cgi_accepted_at TIMESTAMPTZ;
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS cgi_accepted_ip VARCHAR(45);
ALTER TABLE adm_tenants ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS cgi_version VARCHAR(20);

COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.cgi_accepted_at IS 'V6.2.1: Date acceptation CGI/CGU';
COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.cgi_accepted_ip IS 'V6.2.1: IP acceptation CGI/CGU';
COMMENT ON COLUMN adm_tenants.cgi_version IS 'V6.2.1: Version CGI accept√©es (format: YYYY-MM-DD)';

-- 5. Index
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_adm_tenants_stripe_customer
ON adm_tenants(stripe_customer_id) WHERE stripe_customer_id IS NOT NULL;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_adm_tenants_verification_token
ON adm_tenants(verification_token) WHERE verification_token IS NOT NULL;

COMMIT;
```

### 17.3 Migration bil_plans (V6.2.1)

```sql
-- =============================================================================
-- FLEETCORE V6.2.1 - MIGRATION BIL_PLANS
-- Date: 2026-01-06
-- Description: Colonne max_users par forfait

ALTER TABLE bil_plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS max_users INT DEFAULT 5;

COMMENT ON COLUMN bil_plans.max_users IS 'V6.2.1: Nombre max utilisateurs par forfait';

-- Valeurs par d√©faut selon segment
UPDATE bil_plans SET max_users = 1 WHERE code = 'solo';
UPDATE bil_plans SET max_users = 5 WHERE code = 'starter';
UPDATE bil_plans SET max_users = 20 WHERE code = 'pro';
UPDATE bil_plans SET max_users = 9999 WHERE code = 'premium';
```

### 17.4 Migration crm_quotes

```sql
-- Ajout lead_id
ALTER TABLE crm_quotes ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS lead_id UUID REFERENCES crm_leads(id) ON DELETE SET NULL;

-- Contrainte XOR lead/opportunity
ALTER TABLE crm_quotes
  ADD CONSTRAINT crm_quotes_lead_or_opportunity_xor
  CHECK (
    (lead_id IS NOT NULL AND opportunity_id IS NULL) OR
    (lead_id IS NULL AND opportunity_id IS NOT NULL)
  );

-- Index
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_crm_quotes_lead ON crm_quotes(lead_id) WHERE lead_id IS NOT NULL;
```

## 19. CONFIGURATION BIL_SETTINGS V6.2.1

### 19.1 Table bil_settings

```sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bil_settings (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  setting_key VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  setting_value JSONB NOT NULL,
  category VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  data_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'object',
  is_system BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  provider_id UUID REFERENCES adm_providers(id),
  display_label VARCHAR(255),
  description TEXT,
  schema_version VARCHAR(20),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),

  CONSTRAINT bil_settings_category_check CHECK (
    category IN ('payment', 'subscription', 'invoice', 'pricing', 'stripe', 'promotion')
  ),
  CONSTRAINT bil_settings_data_type_check CHECK (
    data_type IN ('object', 'array', 'string', 'number', 'boolean')
  )
);

CREATE INDEX idx_bil_settings_category ON bil_settings(category);

COMMENT ON TABLE bil_settings IS 'V6.2.1: Configuration module Billing';
```

### 19.2 Cl√© `payment_settings`

```json
{
  "version": "6.2.1",
  "payment_link": {
    "allowed_statuses": ["qualified", "demo_completed", "proposal_sent"],
    "expiry_hours": 24,
    "reminder_hours": 12
  },
  "first_month_free": {
    "enabled": true,
    "coupon_id": "FIRST_MONTH_FREE"
  },
  "checkout": {
    "success_path": "/payment-success",
    "cancel_path": "/payment-cancelled"
  },
  "verification": {
    "token_expiry_hours": 24
  }

```

| Module  | P√©rim√®tre                                       | Table settings |
| ------- | ----------------------------------------------- | -------------- |
| **CRM** | Leads, Opportunities, Quotes (AVANT conversion) | `crm_settings` |
| **BIL** | Subscriptions, Invoices, Payments, Stripe       | `bil_settings` |
| **CLT** | Client masterdata, membres (APR√àS conversion)   | -              |
| **ADM** | Tenants, Providers, Config syst√®me              | `adm_settings` |

## 21. M√âTRIQUES ET KPIS

### 21.1 M√©triques Funnel

| M√©trique                   | Formule                            | Target V6.2 |
| -------------------------- | ---------------------------------- | ----------- |
| **Wizard Start Rate**      | Clics CTA / Visiteurs page         | > 5%        |
| **Step 1‚Üí2 Rate**          | Step 2 starts / Step 1 completes   | > 80%       |
| **Step 2‚Üí3 Rate**          | Step 3 starts / Step 2 completes   | > 70%       |
| **Wizard Completion Rate** | Wizard completes / Wizard starts   | > 60%       |
| **Show Rate**              | Appels connect√©s / Bookings        | > 85%       |
| **Confirmation Rate**      | Clics "I'll be there" / Emails J-1 | > 70%       |
| **Qualification Rate**     | Qualified / Appels connect√©s       | > 60%       |
| **Demo-to-Close Rate**     | Converted / Qualified demos        | > 40%       |
| **Overall Conversion**     | Converted / Wizard starts          | > 20%       |
